FROM (
    SELECT c."ComplaintId", c."CategoryId", c."ComplaintCategoryCategoryId", c."ComplaintPriorityPriorityId", c."ComplaintStatusStatusId", c."CreatedAt", c."Description", c."DueDate", c."EmployeeId", c."PriorityId", c."ResolvedAt", c."StatusId", c."Title", c."UserId", e."EmployeeId" AS "EmployeeId0", e."DepartmentId", e."Designation", e."IsActive", e."UserId" AS "UserId0", u."UserId" AS "UserId1", u."Email", u."IsActive" AS "IsActive0", u."JoinedDate", u."Name", u."PasswordHash", u."Phone", u."Role"

    INNER JOIN "Users" AS u ON c."UserId" = u."UserId"

) AS s

    SELECT c."ComplaintId", c."CategoryId", c."ComplaintCategoryCategoryId", c."ComplaintPriorityPriorityId", c."ComplaintStatusStatusId", c."CreatedAt", c."Description", c."DueDate", c."EmployeeId", c."PriorityId", c."ResolvedAt", c."StatusId", c."Title", c."UserId", e."EmployeeId" AS "EmployeeId0", e."DepartmentId", e."Designation", e."IsActive", e."UserId" AS "UserId0", u."UserId" AS "UserId1", u."Email", u."IsActive" AS "IsActive0", u."JoinedDate", u."Name", u."PasswordHash", u."Phone", u."Role"
    FROM "Complaints" AS c
    LEFT JOIN "Employees" AS e ON c."EmployeeId" = e."EmployeeId"
    INNER JOIN "Users" AS u ON c."UserId" = u."UserId"
    WHERE c."ComplaintId" = @complaintId
    LIMIT 1
) AS s
LEFT JOIN "Comments" AS c0 ON s."ComplaintId" = c0."ComplaintId"
LEFT JOIN "ComplaintAttachments" AS c1 ON s."ComplaintId" = c1."ComplaintId"
ORDER BY s."ComplaintId", s."EmployeeId0", s."UserId1", c0."CommentId"

FROM (
    SELECT c."ComplaintId", c."CategoryId", c."ComplaintCategoryCategoryId", c."ComplaintPriorityPriorityId", c."ComplaintStatusStatusId", c."CreatedAt", c."Description", c."DueDate", c."EmployeeId", c."PriorityId", c."ResolvedAt", c."StatusId", c."Title", c."UserId", e."EmployeeId" AS "EmployeeId0", e."DepartmentId", e."Designation", e."IsActive", e."UserId" AS "UserId0", u."UserId" AS "UserId1", u."Email", u."IsActive" AS "IsActive0", u."JoinedDate", u."Name", u."PasswordHash", u."Phone", u."Role"
    FROM "Complaints" AS c
    LEFT JOIN "Employees" AS e ON c."EmployeeId" = e."EmployeeId"
    INNER JOIN "Users" AS u ON c."UserId" = u."UserId"
    WHERE c."ComplaintId" = @complaintId
    LIMIT 1
) AS s
LEFT JOIN "Comments" AS c0 ON s."ComplaintId" = c0."ComplaintId"
LEFT JOIN "ComplaintAttachments" AS c1 ON s."ComplaintId" = c1."ComplaintId"
ORDER BY s."ComplaintId", s."EmployeeId0", s."UserId1", c0."CommentId"
